 antarrashtriya nyaay adaalat (ICJ) ke justise roni abraham ne aadesh diya ki international court ke aakhri faisle tak kulbhushan jadhav kii faansee par roak lagaai jaati he
 Full court hearing
 
 
 - hegg sthit antarrashtriya nyaayalay ke justise roni abraham ne apana faisla padhate hue kaha ki bharat ne bataaya ki kulbhushan jadhav ko pakistan ne giraftaar kiya tha
 After the arrest, India asked for information about Jadhav several times but Pakistan did not provide any information
 - court ne kaha ki bharat ko kulbhushan jadhav maamle main consular acces milanaa chahie
 - The court said that Pakistan has no right to call Kulbhushan Jadhav a spy
 pakistan kaa kulbhushan jadhav ko giraftaar karnaa ek vivaadit mudda he
 - Justice Abraham said that what Pakistan is claiming on Kulbhushan Jadhav is not valid
 - ICJ ne kaha ki court ko kulbhushan jadhav maamle main apana faisla sunaane kaa puraa adhikaar he
 India has placed the matter before the court under the Vienna Treaty
 bharat or pakistan donon deshon ke bich vienna sandhi he, 29 april 1996 ko bharat-paak ne is sandhi par hastakshar kiye the
 - The court said, this decision will be taken under Article 36
 jaj ne kaha ki kulbhushan jadhav maamle main apil sahi samay par daayar nahin kii gai, haalanki donon desh is baat par sahamat hai ki jadhav ek bhartiya naagarik he
 - The court said that the appeal on Jadhav should have been filed within the prescribed limit
 court ko sabhi maamle main hastkshep karne kaa haq nahin he
 However, the court said that the hanging of Kulbhushan Jadhav is banned until the final decision of the International Court of Justice
 - court ne apane faisle me kaha ki bharat kii maang niyamon ke anusaar bilkul sahi he, vienna sandhi ke tahat bharat ko apane naagarik kii madad karne kaa puraa adhikaar he
 - The court said that whatever agreement was reached between India and Pakistan in 2008, it would not be right to implement that agreement under Article 36
 - court ne apana faisla padhate hue saaf taur par kaha ki jab tak international court kaa aakhri faisla nahin aata he, tab tak pakistan kulbhushan jadhav ko puri suraksha muhaiyaa karaaye
 / p> - The court said that India has every right to provide diplomatic, legal aid to its citizens
 - court ne kaha ki bharat ne nivedan kiya he ki international court ke antim faisle tak pakistan kii sarkaar kulbhushan jadhav par koi karrwai naa kare
 - The International Court said that Pakistan had argued that the Vienna Treaty does not apply in this case, but whichever party has been placed by India, it shows that India's side is strong
 - court ne kaha ki bharat ne sanshay jataayaa he ki kulbhushan jadhav ko pakistan main kabhi bhi faansee di ja sakati he, lekin is sanshay par pakistan ne court ko bharosa diya he ki kulbhushan jadhav ko agast 2017 tak faansee nahin di jaaegi

 har namankit vyakti ko yuidi ek aadhaar number degaa

 yuidi databes main vyakti ke sambandh main buniyadi jaankariyaan hongi jaise naam, janm tithi, janm sthaan, ling, mata-pita kaa naam or unke yuidi number, pataa, photo or anguliyon ke nishaan honge
 Unlike PAN card or voter ID card, no benefits or rights can be claimed on the basis of UID number
 isse keval bank khaataa kholane yaa phir mahatma gandhi rashtriya rojgaar guarantee yojana (mgnaraijies yaa naregaa) ke tahat rojgaar jaise kisi kaam ke liye vyakti kii pahchaan karne main madad milegi

 According to a study conducted by the IRIS Knowledge Foundation and the Internet and Mobile Association of India, in the next general election in 2014, social media can affect 160 Lok Sabha seats
 adhyayan main kaha gaya he ki agle aam chunaav main loksabhaa kii kul 543 siton main se 160 ahm siton par soshal media kaa prabhaav rahane kii sambhaavna he, jinamein maharashtra se sabase adhik prabhaav vaali 21 siten or gujarat se 17 siten shaamil he
 The most high-impact seat refers to those seats where the winning margin of the winning candidate in the last Lok Sabha election is less than those using Facebook or the number of voters using Facebook Is 10 percent
 tippaniyan Uttar Pradesh, the largest state in terms of Lok Sabha seats in the country, has 14 such seats, while Karnataka and Tamil Nadu have 12-12, Andhra Pradesh 11 and Kerala 10
 adhyayan ke anusaar, madhya pradesh main aisi siton kii sankhya nau rahegi, jabaki dilli ke saaton loksabhaa kshetron main soshal media kaa prabhaav rahegaa
 The number of such seats in Haryana, Punjab and Rajasthan is five each, while in Chhattisgarh, Bihar, Jammu and Kashmir, Jharkhand and West Bengal, there are four seats each
 adhyayan main 67 siton kii 'atyadhik prabhaav vaali', jabaki shesh siton kii 'kam prabhaav vaali' siton ke rup main pahchaan kii gai he
 The study said that out of the total 543 Lok Sabha seats in the next general election, 160 important seats are likely to have social media influence, including 21 seats with the highest impact from Maharashtra and 17 seats from Gujarat
 sabase adhik prabhaav vaali (hai impact) seat se aashay un siton se he, jahaan pichley loksabhaa chunaav main vijayi ummidavaar ke jeet kaa antar fasebuk kaa prayog karne waalon se kam he athwa jin siton par fasebuk kaa prayog karne waalon kii sankhya kul matadaataaon kii sankhya kaa 10 pratishat he
 The comments desh main loksabhaa siton ke lihaaz se sabase bade rajya uttar pradesh main aisi siton kii sankhya 14 he, jabaki karnataka or tamilnadu main 12-12, andhra pradesh main 11 or kerala main 10 he
 According to the study, the number of such seats in Madhya Pradesh will remain nine, while the social media will have influence in the seven Lok Sabha constituencies of Delhi
 haryana, punjab or rajasthan main aisi siton kii sankhya paanch-paanch he, jabaki chhattisgarh, bihar, jammu evam kashmir, jharkhand or pashchim bengal main aisi chaar-chaar siten hai

 ) After demonetisation, the Modi government has taken another strict step on the old notes of 500 and 1000 rupees

 Ekadashi of Shukla Paksha of Kartik month is called Devauthani Ekadashi
 is baar devuthni ekadshi 8 november ko he
 Devauthani Ekadashi is also known as Hariprabodhini Ekadashi and Devotthan Ekadashi
 mana jaataa he ki bhagwaan vishnu asadha shukla ekadshi ko chaar maah ke liye so jate hai or karthik shukla ekadshi ko jaagate hai
 Chaturmas ends on the day of Devuthani Ekadashi
 kya he devuthni ekadshi kaa mahatv?kaha jaataa he ki in chaar mahino main dev shayan ke kaaran samast mangalik kaary varjit hote hai
 When Mangal (lord Vishnu) wakes up, only then any manglic work is done
 dev jaagran yaa utthan hone ke kaaran isko devotthana ekadshi kehete hai
 Keeping fast on this day is of special importance
 kehete hai isse moksh kii prapti hoti he
 Rules for observing fast on the day of Devuthani Ekadashi- Fasting should be done on waterless or only aquatic substances
 - agar rogi,vruddh,balak,yaa vyast vyakti hai to keval ek bela kaa upwas rakhana chahie
 - Worship Lord Vishnu or your deity
 - tamsik aahaar (pyaaz,lahasun,maance,madiraa,basi bhojan ) bilkul na khaayen
 - On this day, one should chant the mantra "om Namo Bhagwate Vasudevaya Namah"
 - agar aapkaa chandramaa kamjor he yaa maansik samasya he to jal or fal khaakar yaa nirjal ekadshi kaa upwas jarur rakhen
 What is the method of worship of Devuthani Ekadashi? - Build a cane canopy, a square is built in the middle
 - chowk ke madhya main chahen to bhagwaan vishnu kaa chitra yaa murti rakh sakate hai
 - Along with the square, the footprints of God are made, which are covered
 - bhagwaan ko ganna,singhada tathaa fal-mithai samarpit kiya jaataa he
 - a lamp of ghee is lit, which keeps on burning throughout the night
 - bhor main bhagwaan ke charnon kii vidhivat puja kii jaati he or charnon ko sparsh karke unako jagaaya jaataa he
 - shankh-ghanta - and Kirtan is sounded
 - iske baad vrath-upwas kii katha suni jaati he
 After this, all Mars works can be started duly
 - bhagwaan ke charnon kaa sparsh karke jo manokamana kahi jaati he vah puri hoti he
